Feature Flag Definition & Generated Constants\\n\\nThe control begins with the feature flag definition in `pkg/services/featuremgmt/registry.go`, where `ssoSettingsApi` is registered with the description \\\"Enables the SSO settings API and the OAuth configuration UIs in Grafana\\\". API & Authentication Wiring Layer\\n\\n**API Endpoint Registration** in `pkg/services/ssosettings/api/api.go`:\\n\\nThe `Api` struct receives `ssosettings.Service` dependency and registers REST endpoints at the `/api/v1/sso-settings` route group:\\n```go\\nfunc (api *Api) RegisterAPIEndpoints() {\\n  api.RouteRegister.Group(\\\"/api/v1/sso-settings\\\", func(router routing.RouteRegister) {\\n    auth := ac.Middleware(api.AccessControl)\\n    router.Get(\\\"/\\\", auth(ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionSettingsRead)), ...)\\n    router.Get(\\\"/:key\\\", auth(ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionSettingsRead, settingsScope)), ...)\\n    router.Put(\\\"/:key\\\", auth(ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionSettingsWrite, settingsScope)), ...)\\n    router.Delete(\\\"/:key\\\", auth(ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionSettingsWrite, settingsScope)), ...)\\n  })\\n}\\n```\\n\\nEach endpoint is wrapped with access control middleware enforcing:\\n- `ActionSettingsRead` permission for GET operations\\n- `ActionSettingsWrite` permission for PUT/DELETE operations\\n- Scoped to `ScopeSettingsOAuth(\\\":provider\\\")` for provider-specific access control\\n\\n**Service Integration via DI** (`pkg/services/ssosettings/ssosettingsimpl/service.go`):\\n\\nThe `ProvideService` function is the critical integration point that:\\n1. Creates fallback strategies for OAuth, LDAP, and SAML configurations\\n2. **Conditionally enables providers based on feature flags**:\\n   - LDAP added to provider list if `FlagSsoSettingsLDAP` is enabled\\n   - SAML added if enterprise license enables it AND `FlagSsoSettingsSAML` flag is enabled\\n3. **Registers API only when flag is enabled**:\\n   ```go\\n   if features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagSsoSettingsApi) {\\n     ssoSettingsApi := api.ProvideApi(svc, routeRegister, ac)\\n     ssoSettingsApi.RegisterAPIEndpoints()\\n   }\\n   ```\\n\\nThis ensures the REST API infrastructure is only initialized when the feature flag is active.\\n\\n**OAuth Connector Loading** (`pkg/login/social/socialimpl/service.go`):\\n\\nThe `SocialService` receives `ssosettings.Service` as a dependency. In its initialization:\\n```go\\nif s.features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagSsoSettingsApi) {\\n  allSettings, err := ssoSettings.List(context.Background())\\n  // Load OAuth connectors from SSO settings\\n}\\n```\\n\\nWhen enabled, OAuth connectors are loaded from the SSO settings service, enabling dynamic OAuth provider configuration without restart.\\n\\n**LDAP Authentication Registration** (`pkg/services/ldap/service/ldap.go`):\\n\\nThe LDAP service's `ProvideService` function demonstrates the Reloadable integration:\\n```go\\nif s.features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagSsoSettingsApi) && \\n   s.features.IsEnabledGlobally(featuremgmt.FlagSsoSettingsLDAP) {\\n  s.ssoSettings.RegisterReloadable(social.LDAPProviderName, s)\\n}\\n```\\n\\nLDAP registers itself as a Reloadable provider, enabling live LDAP configuration reloading when SSO settings are updated in the database without requiring service restart.\\n\\n### 4. Access Control & Dependency Injection Layer\\n\\n**Access Control Evaluators** (`pkg/services/accesscontrol/ssoutils/utils.go`):\\n\\nTwo evaluators gate access to the SSO settings UI and API:\\n\\n1. **EvalAuthenticationSettings** - for SAML and LDAP:\\n   ```go\\n   func EvalAuthenticationSettings(cfg *setting.Cfg) ac.Evaluator {\\n     return ac.EvalAny(\\n       ac.EvalAll(ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionSettingsWrite, ac.ScopeSettingsSAML),\\n                  ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionSettingsRead, ac.ScopeSettingsSAML)),\\n       ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionLDAPStatusRead))\\n   }\\n   ```\\n\\n2. **OauthSettingsEvaluator** - for OAuth providers:\\n   ```go\\n   func OauthSettingsEvaluator(cfg *setting.Cfg) ac.Evaluator {\\n     result := make([]ac.Evaluator, 0, len(cfg.SSOSettingsConfigurableProviders))\\n     for provider := range cfg.SSOSettingsConfigurableProviders {\\n       result = append(result, ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionSettingsRead, ac.ScopeSettingsOAuth(provider)))\\n       result = append(result, ac.EvalPermission(ac.ActionSettingsWrite, ac.ScopeSettingsOAuth(provider)))\\n     }\\n     return ac.EvalAny(result...)\\n   }\\n   ```\\n\\nThese evaluators build permission checks from the configured providers in `cfg.SSOSettingsConfigurableProviders`.\\n\\n**API Route Protection** (`pkg/api/api.go`):\\n\\nThe admin authentication UI routes demonstrate flag-gated access control:\\n```go\\nadminAuthPageEvaluator := func() ac.Evaluator {\\n  authnSettingsEval :=
